Comando PowerShell ejecutado: powershell -Command "$securePass = ConvertTo-SecureString -String "admin_pass" -AsPlainText -Force; $cred = New-Object -TypeName System.Management.Automation.PSCredential -ArgumentList "admin_user", $securePass; Invoke-Command -ComputerName "ip_destino" -Credential $cred -ScriptBlock { param($targetUser, $newPass); if(Get-LocalUser -Name $targetUser -ErrorAction SilentlyContinue) { Set-LocalUser -Name $targetUser -Password (ConvertTo-SecureString -AsPlainText $newPass -Force); echo 'true'; } else { echo 'false'; } } -ArgumentList "target_user", "user_pass"; "

------INICIO ACCION [2024-03-01 12:17:30]------
 IP Remota del Cliente: 192.168.5.1
  Usuario Administrador: olson
  Contraseña Administrador: 123
  IP del Equipo Remoto: 192.168.5.125
  Usuario Objetivo: 1235
  Nueva Contraseña Usuario: 123
Comando PowerShell ejecutado: powershell -Command "$securePass = ConvertTo-SecureString -String "123" -AsPlainText -Force; $cred = New-Object -TypeName System.Management.Automation.PSCredential -ArgumentList "olson", $securePass; Invoke-Command -ComputerName "192.168.5.125" -Credential $cred -ScriptBlock { param($targetUser, $newPass); if(Get-LocalUser -Name $targetUser -ErrorAction SilentlyContinue) { Set-LocalUser -Name $targetUser -Password (ConvertTo-SecureString -AsPlainText $newPass -Force); echo 'true'; } else { echo 'false'; } } -ArgumentList "1235", "123"; "
